locale wo_rel
  fixes r :: "('a * 'a) set"
  assumes "wo_rel r"
instantiation
  fun :: (type, plus) plus
  plus_fun == plus :: ('a => 'b) => ('a => 'b) => 'a => 'b
instantiation
  fun :: (type, zero) zero
  zero_fun == zero_class.zero :: 'a => 'b

  fun :: (type, times) times

datatype template_term
=
     t_empty
   | template_app of template_term * template_term
   | template_hole of int
   | template_var of int
datatype sign
= equals | greater_equals | greater_than | less_equals | less_than
datatype template
=
     template_bimplication of template * template
   | template_dunno
   | template_equation of template_term * template_term
   | template_implication of template list * template
   | template_inequation of sign * template_term * template_term
   | template_negation of template
   | template_predicate of template_term
constructor t_empty: template_term
constructor template_app: template_term * template_term -> template_term
constructor template_hole: int -> template_term
constructor template_var: int -> template_term
constructor equals: sign
constructor greater_equals: sign
constructor greater_than: sign
constructor less_equals: sign
constructor less_than: sign
constructor template_bimplication: template * template -> template
constructor template_dunno: template
constructor template_equation: template_term * template_term -> template
constructor template_implication: template list * template -> template
constructor template_inequation:
   sign * template_term * template_term -> template
constructor template_negation: template -> template
constructor template_predicate: template_term -> template

  fixes r :: "V"

theorem
  vsvI:
    [| vbrelation ?r;
       !!a b c.
          [| <a, b> \<in>\<^sub>\<circ> ?r; <a, c> \<in>\<^sub>\<circ> ?r |]
          ==> b = c |]
    ==> vsv ?r
theorem
  vsvD:
    vsv ?r ==> vbrelation ?r
    [| vsv ?r; <?a, ?b> \<in>\<^sub>\<circ> ?r;
       <?a, ?c> \<in>\<^sub>\<circ> ?r |]
    ==> ?b = ?c
theorem
  vsvE:
    [| vsv ?r;
       [| vbrelation ?r;
          !!a b c.
             [| <a, b> \<in>\<^sub>\<circ> ?r;
                <a, c> \<in>\<^sub>\<circ> ?r |]
             ==> b = c |]
       ==> ?W |]
    ==> ?W

theorem
  digraphI:
    [| \<Z> ?\<alpha>; vfsequence ?\<CC>; vsv (?\<CC>\<lparr>Dom\<rparr>);
       vsv (?\<CC>\<lparr>Cod\<rparr>); vcard ?\<CC> = 4\<^sub>\<nat>;
       \<D>\<^sub>\<circ> (?\<CC>\<lparr>Dom\<rparr>) =
       ?\<CC>\<lparr>Arr\<rparr>;
       \<R>\<^sub>\<circ> (?\<CC>\<lparr>Dom\<rparr>)
       \<subseteq>\<^sub>\<circ> ?\<CC>\<lparr>Obj\<rparr>;
       \<D>\<^sub>\<circ> (?\<CC>\<lparr>Cod\<rparr>) =
       ?\<CC>\<lparr>Arr\<rparr>;
       \<R>\<^sub>\<circ> (?\<CC>\<lparr>Cod\<rparr>)
       \<subseteq>\<^sub>\<circ> ?\<CC>\<lparr>Obj\<rparr>;
       ?\<CC>\<lparr>Obj\<rparr> \<subseteq>\<^sub>\<circ> Vset ?\<alpha>;
       !!A B.
          [| A \<subseteq>\<^sub>\<circ> ?\<CC>\<lparr>Obj\<rparr>;
             B \<subseteq>\<^sub>\<circ> ?\<CC>\<lparr>Obj\<rparr>;
             A \<in>\<^sub>\<circ> Vset ?\<alpha>;
             B \<in>\<^sub>\<circ> Vset ?\<alpha> |]
          ==> \<Union>\<^sub>\<circ>
               ((\<lambda>a\<in>\<^sub>\<circ>A.
                    \<Union>\<^sub>\<circ>
                     (VLambda B (Hom ?\<CC> a) `\<^sub>\<circ>
                      B)) `\<^sub>\<circ>
                A)
              \<in>\<^sub>\<circ> Vset ?\<alpha> |]
    ==> digraph ?\<alpha> ?\<CC>

locale semicategory
  fixes \<alpha> :: "V"
    and \<CC> :: "V"
  assumes "semicategory \<alpha> \<CC>"
theorem
  semicategoryI:
    [| \<Z> ?\<alpha>; vfsequence ?\<CC>; vsv (?\<CC>\<lparr>Comp\<rparr>);
       vcard ?\<CC> = 5\<^sub>\<nat>; digraph ?\<alpha> (smc_dg ?\<CC>);
       !!gf. (gf \<in>\<^sub>\<circ> \<D>\<^sub>\<circ>
(?\<CC>\<lparr>Comp\<rparr>)) =
             (EX g f b c a.
                 gf = [g, f]\<^sub>\<circ> &
                 g : b \<mapsto>\<^bsub>?\<CC>\<^esub> c &
                 f : a \<mapsto>\<^bsub>?\<CC>\<^esub> b);
       !!b c g a f.
          [| g : b \<mapsto>\<^bsub>?\<CC>\<^esub> c;
             f : a \<mapsto>\<^bsub>?\<CC>\<^esub> b |]
          ==> g \<circ>\<^sub>A\<^bsub>?\<CC>\<^esub>
              f : a \<mapsto>\<^bsub>?\<CC>\<^esub> c;
       !!c d h b g a f.
          [| h : c \<mapsto>\<^bsub>?\<CC>\<^esub> d;
             g : b \<mapsto>\<^bsub>?\<CC>\<^esub> c;
             f : a \<mapsto>\<^bsub>?\<CC>\<^esub> b |]
          ==> h \<circ>\<^sub>A\<^bsub>?\<CC>\<^esub>
              g \<circ>\<^sub>A\<^bsub>?\<CC>\<^esub>
              f =
              h \<circ>\<^sub>A\<^bsub>?\<CC>\<^esub>
              (g \<circ>\<^sub>A\<^bsub>?\<CC>\<^esub> f) |]
    ==> semicategory ?\<alpha> ?\<CC>
theorem
  semicategoryD:
    semicategory ?\<alpha> ?\<CC> ==> \<Z> ?\<alpha>
    semicategory ?\<alpha> ?\<CC> ==> vfsequence ?\<CC>
    semicategory ?\<alpha> ?\<CC> ==> vsv (?\<CC>\<lparr>Comp\<rparr>)
    semicategory ?\<alpha> ?\<CC> ==> vcard ?\<CC> = 5\<^sub>\<nat>
    semicategory ?\<alpha> ?\<CC> ==> digraph ?\<alpha> (smc_dg ?\<CC>)
    semicategory ?\<alpha> ?\<CC> ==>
    (?gf
     \<in>\<^sub>\<circ> \<D>\<^sub>\<circ> (?\<CC>\<lparr>Comp\<rparr>)) =
    (EX g f b c a.
        ?gf = [g, f]\<^sub>\<circ> &
        g : b \<mapsto>\<^bsub>?\<CC>\<^esub> c &
        f : a \<mapsto>\<^bsub>?\<CC>\<^esub> b)
    [| semicategory ?\<alpha> ?\<CC>;
       ?g : ?b \<mapsto>\<^bsub>?\<CC>\<^esub> ?c;
       ?f : ?a \<mapsto>\<^bsub>?\<CC>\<^esub> ?b |]
    ==> ?g \<circ>\<^sub>A\<^bsub>?\<CC>\<^esub>
        ?f : ?a \<mapsto>\<^bsub>?\<CC>\<^esub> ?c
    [| semicategory ?\<alpha> ?\<CC>;
       ?h : ?c \<mapsto>\<^bsub>?\<CC>\<^esub> ?d;
       ?g : ?b \<mapsto>\<^bsub>?\<CC>\<^esub> ?c;
       ?f : ?a \<mapsto>\<^bsub>?\<CC>\<^esub> ?b |]
    ==> ?h \<circ>\<^sub>A\<^bsub>?\<CC>\<^esub>
        ?g \<circ>\<^sub>A\<^bsub>?\<CC>\<^esub>
        ?f =
        ?h \<circ>\<^sub>A\<^bsub>?\<CC>\<^esub>
        (?g \<circ>\<^sub>A\<^bsub>?\<CC>\<^esub> ?f)

theorem
  pdigraphI:
    [| pdigraph_base ?\<alpha> ?I ?\<AA>;
       !!J. J \<subseteq>\<^sub>\<circ> ?I ==>
            dg_prod J ?\<AA>\<lparr>Obj\<rparr>
            \<subseteq>\<^sub>\<circ> Vset ?\<alpha>;
       !!J A B.
          [| J \<subseteq>\<^sub>\<circ> ?I;
             A \<subseteq>\<^sub>\<circ> dg_prod J
    ?\<AA>\<lparr>Obj\<rparr>;
             B \<subseteq>\<^sub>\<circ> dg_prod J

             A \<in>\<^sub>\<circ> Vset ?\<alpha>;
             B \<in>\<^sub>\<circ> Vset ?\<alpha> |]
          ==> \<Union>\<^sub>\<circ>
               ((\<lambda>a\<in>\<^sub>\<circ>A.
                    \<Union>\<^sub>\<circ>
                     (VLambda B (Hom (dg_prod J ?\<AA>) a) `\<^sub>\<circ>
                      B)) `\<^sub>\<circ>
                A)
              \<in>\<^sub>\<circ> Vset ?\<alpha> |]
    ==> pdigraph ?\<alpha> ?I ?\<AA>

             A \<in>\<^sub>\<circ> Vset ?\<alpha>;
             B \<in>\<^sub>\<circ> Vset ?\<alpha> |]
          ==> \<Union>\<^sub>\<circ>
               ((\<lambda>a\<in>\<^sub>\<circ>A.
                    \<Union>\<^sub>\<circ>
                     (VLambda B (Hom (smc_prod J ?\<AA>) a) `\<^sub>\<circ>
                      B)) `\<^sub>\<circ>
                A)
              \<in>\<^sub>\<circ> Vset ?\<alpha> |]
    ==> psemicategory ?\<alpha> ?I ?\<AA>
theorem
  psemicategoryD:
    psemicategory ?\<alpha> ?I ?\<AA> ==>
    psemicategory_base ?\<alpha> ?I ?\<AA>
    [| psemicategory ?\<alpha> ?I ?\<AA>; ?J \<subseteq>\<^sub>\<circ> ?I |]
    ==> smc_prod ?J ?\<AA>\<lparr>Obj\<rparr>
        \<subseteq>\<^sub>\<circ> Vset ?\<alpha>
    [| psemicategory ?\<alpha> ?I ?\<AA>; ?J \<subseteq>\<^sub>\<circ> ?I;
       ?A \<subseteq>\<^sub>\<circ> smc_prod ?J ?\<AA>\<lparr>Obj\<rparr>;
       ?B \<subseteq>\<^sub>\<circ> smc_prod ?J ?\<AA>\<lparr>Obj\<rparr>;
       ?A \<in>\<^sub>\<circ> Vset ?\<alpha>;
       ?B \<in>\<^sub>\<circ> Vset ?\<alpha> |]
    ==> \<Union>\<^sub>\<circ>
         ((\<lambda>a\<in>\<^sub>\<circ>?A.
              \<Union>\<^sub>\<circ>
               (VLambda ?B (Hom (smc_prod ?J ?\<AA>) a) `\<^sub>\<circ>
                ?B)) `\<^sub>\<circ>
          ?A)
        \<in>\<^sub>\<circ> Vset ?\<alpha>
theorem
  psemicategoryE:
    [| psemicategory ?\<alpha> ?I ?\<AA>;
       [| psemicategory_base ?\<alpha> ?I ?\<AA>;
          !!J. J \<subseteq>\<^sub>\<circ> ?I ==>
               smc_prod J ?\<AA>\<lparr>Obj\<rparr>
               \<subseteq>\<^sub>\<circ> Vset ?\<alpha>;
          !!J A B.
             [| J \<subseteq>\<^sub>\<circ> ?I;
                A \<subseteq>\<^sub>\<circ> smc_prod J
       ?\<AA>\<lparr>Obj\<rparr>;
                B \<subseteq>\<^sub>\<circ> smc_prod J
       ?\<AA>\<lparr>Obj\<rparr>;
                A \<in>\<^sub>\<circ> Vset ?\<alpha>;
                B \<in>\<^sub>\<circ> Vset ?\<alpha> |]
             ==> \<Union>\<^sub>\<circ>
                  ((\<lambda>a\<in>\<^sub>\<circ>A.
                       \<Union>\<^sub>\<circ>
                        (VLambda B
                          (Hom (smc_prod J ?\<AA>) a) `\<^sub>\<circ>
                         B)) `\<^sub>\<circ>
                   A)
                 \<in>\<^sub>\<circ> Vset ?\<alpha> |]
       ==> ?W |]
    ==> ?W
locale psemicategory
  fixes \<alpha> :: "V"
    and I :: "V"
    and \<AA> :: "V => V"
  assumes "psemicategory \<alpha> I \<AA>"
locale finite_psemicategory
  fixes \<alpha> :: "V"
    and I :: "V"
    and \<AA> :: "V => V"
  assumes "finite_psemicategory \<alpha> I \<AA>"
theorem
  finite_psemicategoryI:
    [| psemicategory_base ?\<alpha> ?I ?\<AA>; vfinite ?I |]
    ==> finite_psemicategory ?\<alpha> ?I ?\<AA>
locale subsemicategory
  fixes \<alpha> :: "V"
    and \<BB> :: "V"
    and \<CC> :: "V"
  assumes
    "\<BB>
     \<subseteq>\<^sub>S\<^sub>M\<^sub>C\<^bsub>\<alpha>\<^esub> \<CC>"
theorem
  finite_psemicategoryD:
    finite_psemicategory ?\<alpha> ?I ?\<AA> ==>
    psemicategory_base ?\<alpha> ?I ?\<AA>
    finite_psemicategory ?\<alpha> ?I ?\<AA> ==> vfinite ?I
theorem
  finite_psemicategoryE:
    [| finite_psemicategory ?\<alpha> ?I ?\<AA>;
       [| psemicategory_base ?\<alpha> ?I ?\<AA>; vfinite ?I |] ==> ?W |]
    ==> ?W
theorem
  is_ntsmcfI:
    [| \<Z> ?\<alpha>; vfsequence ?\<NN>;
       ?\<FF> :
       ?\<AA> \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>S\<^sub>M\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<BB>;
       ?\<GG> :
       ?\<AA> \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>S\<^sub>M\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<BB>;
       vcard ?\<NN> = 5\<^sub>\<nat>;
       ntsmcf_tdghm ?\<NN> :
       smcf_dghm
        ?\<FF> \<mapsto>\<^sub>D\<^sub>G\<^sub>H\<^sub>M smcf_dghm ?\<GG> :
       smc_dg
        ?\<AA> \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>D\<^sub>G\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> smc_dg
?\<BB>;
       ?\<NN>\<lparr>NTDom\<rparr> = ?\<FF>;
       ?\<NN>\<lparr>NTCod\<rparr> = ?\<GG>;
       ?\<NN>\<lparr>NTDGDom\<rparr> = ?\<AA>;
       ?\<NN>\<lparr>NTDGCod\<rparr> = ?\<BB>;
       !!a b f.
          f : a \<mapsto>\<^bsub>?\<AA>\<^esub> b ==>
          ?\<NN>\<lparr>NTMap\<rparr>\<lparr>b\<rparr> \<circ>\<^sub>A\<^bsub>?\<BB>\<^esub>
          ?\<FF>\<lparr>ArrMap\<rparr>\<lparr>f\<rparr> =
          ?\<GG>\<lparr>ArrMap\<rparr>\<lparr>f\<rparr> \<circ>\<^sub>A\<^bsub>?\<BB>\<^esub>
          ?\<NN>\<lparr>NTMap\<rparr>\<lparr>a\<rparr> |]
    ==> ?\<NN> : ?\<FF> \<mapsto>\<^sub>S\<^sub>M\<^sub>C\<^sub>F ?\<GG> :
        ?\<AA> \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>S\<^sub>M\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<BB>

    ?\<NN> : ?\<FF> \<mapsto>\<^sub>S\<^sub>M\<^sub>C\<^sub>F ?\<GG> :

    ?\<NN> : ?\<FF> \<mapsto>\<^sub>S\<^sub>M\<^sub>C\<^sub>F ?\<GG> :

     ?\<AA> \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>D\<^sub>G\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> smc_dg
                                   ?\<BB>
    ?\<NN> : ?\<FF> \<mapsto>\<^sub>S\<^sub>M\<^sub>C\<^sub>F ?\<GG> :
    ?\<AA> \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>S\<^sub>M\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<BB> ==>

    ?\<AA> \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>S\<^sub>M\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<BB> ==>

        ?\<NN>\<lparr>NTMap\<rparr>\<lparr>?a\<rparr>

        ?\<AA> \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<BB>

theorem
  ntsmcf_smcf_comp_NTMap_vdomain:
    \<D>\<^sub>\<circ>
     ((?\<NN> \<circ>\<^sub>T\<^sub>D\<^sub>G\<^sub>H\<^sub>M\<^sub>-\<^sub>D\<^sub>G\<^sub>H\<^sub>M
       \<FF>)\<lparr>NTMap\<rparr>) =
    \<AA>\<lparr>Obj\<rparr>
theorem
  ntsmcf_smcf_comp_NTMap_app:
    ?x \<in>\<^sub>\<circ> \<AA>\<lparr>Obj\<rparr> ==>

locale cat_parallel
  fixes \<alpha> :: "V"
    and \<aa> :: "V"
    and \<bb> :: "V"
    and \<gg> :: "V"
    and \<ff> :: "V"
  assumes "cat_parallel \<alpha> \<aa> \<bb> \<gg> \<ff>"
theorem
  cat_parallelI:
    [| \<Z> ?\<alpha>; ?\<aa> ~= ?\<bb>; ?\<aa> ~= ?\<gg>; ?\<aa> ~= ?\<ff>;
       ?\<bb> ~= ?\<gg>; ?\<bb> ~= ?\<ff>; ?\<gg> ~= ?\<ff>;
       ?\<aa> \<in>\<^sub>\<circ> Vset ?\<alpha>;
       ?\<bb> \<in>\<^sub>\<circ> Vset ?\<alpha>;
       ?\<gg> \<in>\<^sub>\<circ> Vset ?\<alpha>;
       ?\<ff> \<in>\<^sub>\<circ> Vset ?\<alpha> |]
    ==> cat_parallel ?\<alpha> ?\<aa> ?\<bb> ?\<gg> ?\<ff>
theorem
  cat_parallelD:
    cat_parallel ?\<alpha> ?\<aa> ?\<bb> ?\<gg> ?\<ff> ==> \<Z> ?\<alpha>
    cat_parallel ?\<alpha> ?\<aa> ?\<bb> ?\<gg> ?\<ff> ==> ?\<aa> ~= ?\<bb>
    cat_parallel ?\<alpha> ?\<aa> ?\<bb> ?\<gg> ?\<ff> ==> ?\<aa> ~= ?\<gg>
    cat_parallel ?\<alpha> ?\<aa> ?\<bb> ?\<gg> ?\<ff> ==> ?\<aa> ~= ?\<ff>
    cat_parallel ?\<alpha> ?\<aa> ?\<bb> ?\<gg> ?\<ff> ==> ?\<bb> ~= ?\<gg>
    cat_parallel ?\<alpha> ?\<aa> ?\<bb> ?\<gg> ?\<ff> ==> ?\<bb> ~= ?\<ff>
    cat_parallel ?\<alpha> ?\<aa> ?\<bb> ?\<gg> ?\<ff> ==> ?\<gg> ~= ?\<ff>
    cat_parallel ?\<alpha> ?\<aa> ?\<bb> ?\<gg> ?\<ff> ==>
    ?\<aa> \<in>\<^sub>\<circ> Vset ?\<alpha>
    cat_parallel ?\<alpha> ?\<aa> ?\<bb> ?\<gg> ?\<ff> ==>
    ?\<bb> \<in>\<^sub>\<circ> Vset ?\<alpha>
    cat_parallel ?\<alpha> ?\<aa> ?\<bb> ?\<gg> ?\<ff> ==>
    ?\<gg> \<in>\<^sub>\<circ> Vset ?\<alpha>
    cat_parallel ?\<alpha> ?\<aa> ?\<bb> ?\<gg> ?\<ff> ==>
    ?\<ff> \<in>\<^sub>\<circ> Vset ?\<alpha>

  fixes \<alpha> :: "V"

  pcategoryI:
    [| pcategory_base ?\<alpha> ?I ?\<AA>;
       !!J. J \<subseteq>\<^sub>\<circ> ?I ==>
            cat_prod J ?\<AA>\<lparr>Obj\<rparr>
            \<subseteq>\<^sub>\<circ> Vset ?\<alpha>;

             A \<subseteq>\<^sub>\<circ> cat_prod J

                         B)) `\<^sub>\<circ>
                   A)
                 \<in>\<^sub>\<circ> Vset ?\<alpha> |]
       ==> ?W |]
    ==> ?W

       [| ?u :
          ?\<FF> >\<^sub>C\<^sub>F\<^sub>.\<^sub>c\<^sub>o\<^sub>c\<^sub>o\<^sub>n\<^sub>e ?r :
          ?\<JJ> \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<CC>;
          !!u' r'.
             u' :
             ?\<FF> >\<^sub>C\<^sub>F\<^sub>.\<^sub>c\<^sub>o\<^sub>c\<^sub>o\<^sub>n\<^sub>e r' :
             ?\<JJ> \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<CC> ==>
             EX! f'.
                f' : ?r \<mapsto>\<^bsub>?\<CC>\<^esub> r' &
                u' =
                ntcf_const ?\<JJ> ?\<CC>
                 f' \<bullet>\<^sub>N\<^sub>T\<^sub>S\<^sub>M\<^sub>C\<^sub>F
                ?u |]
       ==> ?W |]
    ==> ?W
locale is_cf_adjunction
  fixes \<alpha> :: "V"
    and \<CC> :: "V"
    and \<DD> :: "V"
    and \<FF> :: "V"
    and \<GG> :: "V"
    and \<Phi> :: "V"
  assumes "is_cf_adjunction \<alpha> \<CC> \<DD> \<FF> \<GG> \<Phi>"
theorem
  is_cf_adjunctionI:
    [| \<Z> ?\<alpha>; vfsequence ?\<Phi>; category ?\<alpha> ?\<CC>;
       category ?\<alpha> ?\<DD>;
       ?\<FF> :
       ?\<CC> \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<DD>;
       ?\<GG> :
       ?\<DD> \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<CC>;
       ?\<Phi>\<lparr>AdjNT\<rparr> : Hom\<^sub>O\<^sub>.\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub>?\<DD>(
       ?\<FF>-,-
       ) \<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^sub>F\<^sub>.\<^sub>i\<^sub>s\<^sub>o Hom\<^sub>O\<^sub>.\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub>?\<CC>(
       -,?\<GG>-
       ) : op_cat ?\<CC> \<times>\<^sub>C
           ?\<DD> \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> cat_Set
                                 ?\<alpha>;
       vcard ?\<Phi> = 3\<^sub>\<nat>;
       ?\<Phi>\<lparr>AdjLeft\<rparr> = ?\<FF>;
       ?\<Phi>\<lparr>AdjRight\<rparr> = ?\<GG> |]
    ==> ?\<Phi> : ?\<FF> \<rightleftharpoons>\<^sub>C\<^sub>F ?\<GG> : ?\<CC> \<rightleftharpoons>\<rightleftharpoons>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<DD>
theorem
  is_cf_adjunctionD:
    ?\<Phi> : ?\<FF> \<rightleftharpoons>\<^sub>C\<^sub>F ?\<GG> : ?\<CC> \<rightleftharpoons>\<rightleftharpoons>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<DD> ==>
    \<Z> ?\<alpha>
    ?\<Phi> : ?\<FF> \<rightleftharpoons>\<^sub>C\<^sub>F ?\<GG> : ?\<CC> \<rightleftharpoons>\<rightleftharpoons>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<DD> ==>
    vfsequence ?\<Phi>
    ?\<Phi> : ?\<FF> \<rightleftharpoons>\<^sub>C\<^sub>F ?\<GG> : ?\<CC> \<rightleftharpoons>\<rightleftharpoons>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<DD> ==>
    category ?\<alpha> ?\<CC>
    ?\<Phi> : ?\<FF> \<rightleftharpoons>\<^sub>C\<^sub>F ?\<GG> : ?\<CC> \<rightleftharpoons>\<rightleftharpoons>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<DD> ==>
    category ?\<alpha> ?\<DD>
    ?\<Phi> : ?\<FF> \<rightleftharpoons>\<^sub>C\<^sub>F ?\<GG> : ?\<CC> \<rightleftharpoons>\<rightleftharpoons>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<DD> ==>
    ?\<FF> :
    ?\<CC> \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<DD>
    ?\<Phi> : ?\<FF> \<rightleftharpoons>\<^sub>C\<^sub>F ?\<GG> : ?\<CC> \<rightleftharpoons>\<rightleftharpoons>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<DD> ==>
    ?\<GG> :
    ?\<DD> \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<CC>
    ?\<Phi> : ?\<FF> \<rightleftharpoons>\<^sub>C\<^sub>F ?\<GG> : ?\<CC> \<rightleftharpoons>\<rightleftharpoons>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<DD> ==>
    ?\<Phi>\<lparr>AdjNT\<rparr> : Hom\<^sub>O\<^sub>.\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub>?\<DD>(
    ?\<FF>-,-
    ) \<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^sub>F\<^sub>.\<^sub>i\<^sub>s\<^sub>o Hom\<^sub>O\<^sub>.\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub>?\<CC>(
    -,?\<GG>-
    ) : op_cat ?\<CC> \<times>\<^sub>C
        ?\<DD> \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> cat_Set
                              ?\<alpha>
    ?\<Phi> : ?\<FF> \<rightleftharpoons>\<^sub>C\<^sub>F ?\<GG> : ?\<CC> \<rightleftharpoons>\<rightleftharpoons>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<DD> ==>
    vcard ?\<Phi> = 3\<^sub>\<nat>
    ?\<Phi> : ?\<FF> \<rightleftharpoons>\<^sub>C\<^sub>F ?\<GG> : ?\<CC> \<rightleftharpoons>\<rightleftharpoons>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<DD> ==>
    ?\<Phi>\<lparr>AdjLeft\<rparr> = ?\<FF>
    ?\<Phi> : ?\<FF> \<rightleftharpoons>\<^sub>C\<^sub>F ?\<GG> : ?\<CC> \<rightleftharpoons>\<rightleftharpoons>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<DD> ==>
    ?\<Phi>\<lparr>AdjRight\<rparr> = ?\<GG>
theorem
  is_cf_adjunctionE:
    [| ?\<Phi> : ?\<FF> \<rightleftharpoons>\<^sub>C\<^sub>F ?\<GG> : ?\<CC> \<rightleftharpoons>\<rightleftharpoons>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<DD>;
       [| \<Z> ?\<alpha>; vfsequence ?\<Phi>; category ?\<alpha> ?\<CC>;
          category ?\<alpha> ?\<DD>;
          ?\<FF> :
          ?\<CC> \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<DD>;
          ?\<GG> :
          ?\<DD> \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<CC>;
          ?\<Phi>\<lparr>AdjNT\<rparr> : Hom\<^sub>O\<^sub>.\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub>?\<DD>(
          ?\<FF>-,-
          ) \<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^sub>F\<^sub>.\<^sub>i\<^sub>s\<^sub>o Hom\<^sub>O\<^sub>.\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub>?\<CC>(
          -,?\<GG>-
          ) : op_cat ?\<CC> \<times>\<^sub>C
              ?\<DD> \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> cat_Set
                                    ?\<alpha>;
          vcard ?\<Phi> = 3\<^sub>\<nat>;
          ?\<Phi>\<lparr>AdjLeft\<rparr> = ?\<FF>;
          ?\<Phi>\<lparr>AdjRight\<rparr> = ?\<GG> |]
       ==> ?W |]
    ==> ?W
locale is_cat_finite_limit
  fixes \<alpha> :: "V"
    and \<JJ> :: "V"
    and \<CC> :: "V"
    and \<FF> :: "V"
    and r :: "V"
    and u :: "V"
  assumes "is_cat_finite_limit \<alpha> \<JJ> \<CC> \<FF> r u"
locale is_cat_finite_colimit
  fixes \<alpha> :: "V"
    and \<JJ> :: "V"
    and \<CC> :: "V"
    and \<FF> :: "V"
    and r :: "V"
    and u :: "V"
  assumes "is_cat_finite_colimit \<alpha> \<JJ> \<CC> \<FF> r u"
theorem
  is_cat_finite_limitI:
    [| ?u : ?r <\<^sub>C\<^sub>F\<^sub>.\<^sub>l\<^sub>i\<^sub>m ?\<FF> :
       ?\<JJ> \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<CC>;
       finite_category ?\<alpha> ?\<JJ> |]
    ==> ?u :
        ?r <\<^sub>C\<^sub>F\<^sub>.\<^sub>l\<^sub>i\<^sub>m\<^sub>.\<^sub>f\<^sub>i\<^sub>n ?\<FF> :
        ?\<JJ> \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<CC>
theorem
  is_cat_finite_limitD:
    ?u :
    ?r <\<^sub>C\<^sub>F\<^sub>.\<^sub>l\<^sub>i\<^sub>m\<^sub>.\<^sub>f\<^sub>i\<^sub>n ?\<FF> :
    ?\<JJ> \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<CC> ==>
    ?u : ?r <\<^sub>C\<^sub>F\<^sub>.\<^sub>l\<^sub>i\<^sub>m ?\<FF> :
    ?\<JJ> \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<CC>
    ?u :
    ?r <\<^sub>C\<^sub>F\<^sub>.\<^sub>l\<^sub>i\<^sub>m\<^sub>.\<^sub>f\<^sub>i\<^sub>n ?\<FF> :
    ?\<JJ> \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<CC> ==>
    finite_category ?\<alpha> ?\<JJ>
theorem
  is_cat_finite_limitE:
    [| ?u :
       ?r <\<^sub>C\<^sub>F\<^sub>.\<^sub>l\<^sub>i\<^sub>m\<^sub>.\<^sub>f\<^sub>i\<^sub>n ?\<FF> :
       ?\<JJ> \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<CC>;
       [| ?u : ?r <\<^sub>C\<^sub>F\<^sub>.\<^sub>l\<^sub>i\<^sub>m ?\<FF> :
          ?\<JJ> \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<CC>;
          finite_category ?\<alpha> ?\<JJ> |]
       ==> ?W |]
    ==> ?W
theorem
  is_cat_finite_colimitI:
    [| ?u :
       ?\<FF> >\<^sub>C\<^sub>F\<^sub>.\<^sub>c\<^sub>o\<^sub>l\<^sub>i\<^sub>m ?r :
       ?\<JJ> \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<CC>;

    ==> ?u :
        ?\<FF> >\<^sub>C\<^sub>F\<^sub>.\<^sub>c\<^sub>o\<^sub>l\<^sub>i\<^sub>m\<^sub>.\<^sub>f\<^sub>i\<^sub>n ?r :

    ?u :

    ?\<JJ> \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<CC> ==>
    ?u :
    ?\<FF> >\<^sub>C\<^sub>F\<^sub>.\<^sub>c\<^sub>o\<^sub>l\<^sub>i\<^sub>m ?r :
    ?\<JJ> \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<CC>
    ?u :
    ?\<FF> >\<^sub>C\<^sub>F\<^sub>.\<^sub>c\<^sub>o\<^sub>l\<^sub>i\<^sub>m\<^sub>.\<^sub>f\<^sub>i\<^sub>n ?r :
    ?\<JJ> \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<CC> ==>
    finite_category ?\<alpha> ?\<JJ>
theorem
  is_cat_finite_colimitE:
    [| ?u :
       ?\<FF> >\<^sub>C\<^sub>F\<^sub>.\<^sub>c\<^sub>o\<^sub>l\<^sub>i\<^sub>m\<^sub>.\<^sub>f\<^sub>i\<^sub>n ?r :
       ?\<JJ> \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<CC>;
       [| ?u :
          ?\<FF> >\<^sub>C\<^sub>F\<^sub>.\<^sub>c\<^sub>o\<^sub>l\<^sub>i\<^sub>m ?r :
          ?\<JJ> \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<CC>;
          finite_category ?\<alpha> ?\<JJ> |]
       ==> ?W |]

locale is_cf_adjunction
  fixes \<alpha> :: "V"
    and \<CC> :: "V"
    and \<DD> :: "V"
    and \<FF> :: "V"
    and \<GG> :: "V"
    and \<Phi> :: "V"
  assumes
    "\<Phi> : \<FF> \<rightleftharpoons>\<^sub>C\<^sub>F \<GG> : \<CC> \<rightleftharpoons>\<rightleftharpoons>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>\<alpha>\<^esub> \<DD>"
theorem
  cf_adjunction_unit_NTMap_vdomain:
    \<D>\<^sub>\<circ> (\<eta>\<^sub>C \<Phi>\<lparr>NTMap\<rparr>) =
    \<CC>\<lparr>Obj\<rparr>
theorem
  cf_adjunction_unit_NTMap_app:
    ?x \<in>\<^sub>\<circ> \<CC>\<lparr>Obj\<rparr> ==>
    \<eta>\<^sub>C \<Phi>\<lparr>NTMap\<rparr>\<lparr>?x\<rparr> =
    (\<Phi>\<lparr>AdjNT\<rparr>\<lparr>NTMap\<rparr> \<lparr>?x,
                        \<FF>\<lparr>ObjMap\<rparr>\<lparr>?x\<rparr>\<rparr>\<^sub>\<bullet>)\<lparr>ArrVal\<rparr>\<lparr>\<DD>\<lparr>CId\<rparr>\<lparr>\<FF>\<lparr>ObjMap\<rparr>\<lparr>?x\<rparr>\<rparr>\<rparr>
theorem
  cf_adjunction_unit_NTMap_vsv:
    vsv (\<eta>\<^sub>C ?\<Phi>\<lparr>NTMap\<rparr>)
locale is_cat_obj_prod
  fixes \<alpha> :: "V"
    and I :: "V"
    and A :: "V => V"
    and \<CC> :: "V"
    and P :: "V"
    and \<pi> :: "V"
  assumes "is_cat_obj_prod \<alpha> I A \<CC> P \<pi>"
locale is_cat_obj_coprod
  fixes \<alpha> :: "V"
    and I :: "V"
    and A :: "V => V"
    and \<CC> :: "V"
    and U :: "V"
    and \<pi> :: "V"
  assumes "is_cat_obj_coprod \<alpha> I A \<CC> U \<pi>"
theorem
  is_cat_obj_prodI:
    [| ?\<pi> :
       ?P <\<^sub>C\<^sub>F\<^sub>.\<^sub>l\<^sub>i\<^sub>m :\<rightarrow>:
                       ?I ?A ?\<CC> :
       :\<^sub>C
        ?I \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<CC>;
       cf_discrete ?\<alpha> ?I ?A ?\<CC> |]
    ==> ?\<pi> : ?P <\<^sub>C\<^sub>F\<^sub>.\<^sub>\<Prod> ?A :
        ?I \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<CC>
theorem
  is_cat_obj_prodD:
    ?\<pi> : ?P <\<^sub>C\<^sub>F\<^sub>.\<^sub>\<Prod> ?A :
    ?I \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<CC> ==>
    ?\<pi> :
    ?P <\<^sub>C\<^sub>F\<^sub>.\<^sub>l\<^sub>i\<^sub>m :\<rightarrow>: ?I
                    ?A ?\<CC> :
    :\<^sub>C ?I \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<CC>
    ?\<pi> : ?P <\<^sub>C\<^sub>F\<^sub>.\<^sub>\<Prod> ?A :
    ?I \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<CC> ==>
    cf_discrete ?\<alpha> ?I ?A ?\<CC>
theorem
  is_cat_obj_prodE:
    [| ?\<pi> : ?P <\<^sub>C\<^sub>F\<^sub>.\<^sub>\<Prod> ?A :
       ?I \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<CC>;
       [| ?\<pi> :
          ?P <\<^sub>C\<^sub>F\<^sub>.\<^sub>l\<^sub>i\<^sub>m :\<rightarrow>:
                          ?I ?A ?\<CC> :
          :\<^sub>C
           ?I \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<CC>;
          cf_discrete ?\<alpha> ?I ?A ?\<CC> |]
       ==> ?W |]
    ==> ?W
theorem
  is_cat_obj_coprodI:
    [| ?\<pi> :
       :\<rightarrow>: ?I ?A
        ?\<CC> >\<^sub>C\<^sub>F\<^sub>.\<^sub>c\<^sub>o\<^sub>l\<^sub>i\<^sub>m ?U :
       :\<^sub>C
        ?I \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<CC>;
       cf_discrete ?\<alpha> ?I ?A ?\<CC> |]
    ==> ?\<pi> : ?A >\<^sub>C\<^sub>F\<^sub>.\<^sub>\<Coprod> ?U :
        ?I \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<CC>
theorem
  is_cat_obj_coprodD:
    ?\<pi> : ?A >\<^sub>C\<^sub>F\<^sub>.\<^sub>\<Coprod> ?U :
    ?I \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<CC> ==>
    ?\<pi> :
    :\<rightarrow>: ?I ?A
     ?\<CC> >\<^sub>C\<^sub>F\<^sub>.\<^sub>c\<^sub>o\<^sub>l\<^sub>i\<^sub>m ?U :
    :\<^sub>C ?I \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<CC>
    ?\<pi> : ?A >\<^sub>C\<^sub>F\<^sub>.\<^sub>\<Coprod> ?U :
    ?I \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<CC> ==>
    cf_discrete ?\<alpha> ?I ?A ?\<CC>
theorem
  is_cat_obj_coprodE:
    [| ?\<pi> : ?A >\<^sub>C\<^sub>F\<^sub>.\<^sub>\<Coprod> ?U :
       ?I \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<CC>;
       [| ?\<pi> :
          :\<rightarrow>: ?I ?A
           ?\<CC> >\<^sub>C\<^sub>F\<^sub>.\<^sub>c\<^sub>o\<^sub>l\<^sub>i\<^sub>m ?U :
          :\<^sub>C
           ?I \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<CC>;
          cf_discrete ?\<alpha> ?I ?A ?\<CC> |]
       ==> ?W |]
    ==> ?W
locale is_cf_adjunction
  fixes \<alpha> :: "V"
    and \<CC> :: "V"
    and \<DD> :: "V"
    and \<FF> :: "V"
    and \<GG> :: "V"
    and \<Phi> :: "V"
  assumes
    "\<Phi> : \<FF> \<rightleftharpoons>\<^sub>C\<^sub>F \<GG> : \<CC> \<rightleftharpoons>\<rightleftharpoons>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>\<alpha>\<^esub> \<DD>"
theorem
  cf_adjunction_counit_NTMap_vdomain:
    \<D>\<^sub>\<circ> (\<epsilon>\<^sub>C \<Phi>\<lparr>NTMap\<rparr>) =
    \<DD>\<lparr>Obj\<rparr>
theorem
  cf_adjunction_counit_NTMap_app:
    ?x \<in>\<^sub>\<circ> \<DD>\<lparr>Obj\<rparr> ==>
    \<epsilon>\<^sub>C \<Phi>\<lparr>NTMap\<rparr>\<lparr>?x\<rparr> =
    (\<Phi>\<lparr>AdjNT\<rparr>\<lparr>NTMap\<rparr> \<lparr>\<GG>\<lparr>ObjMap\<rparr>\<lparr>?x\<rparr>,
                        ?x\<rparr>\<^sub>\<bullet>)\<inverse>\<^sub>R\<^sub>e\<^sub>l\<lparr>ArrVal\<rparr>\<lparr>\<CC>\<lparr>CId\<rparr>\<lparr>\<GG>\<lparr>ObjMap\<rparr>\<lparr>?x\<rparr>\<rparr>\<rparr>
theorem
  cf_adjunction_counit_NTMap_vsv:
    vsv (\<epsilon>\<^sub>C ?\<Phi>\<lparr>NTMap\<rparr>)
locale is_cat_finite_obj_prod
  fixes \<alpha> :: "V"
    and I :: "V"
    and A :: "V => V"
    and \<CC> :: "V"
    and P :: "V"
    and \<pi> :: "V"
  assumes "is_cat_finite_obj_prod \<alpha> I A \<CC> P \<pi>"
locale is_cat_finite_obj_coprod
  fixes \<alpha> :: "V"
    and I :: "V"
    and A :: "V => V"
    and \<CC> :: "V"
    and U :: "V"
    and \<pi> :: "V"
  assumes "is_cat_finite_obj_coprod \<alpha> I A \<CC> U \<pi>"
theorem
  is_cat_finite_obj_prodI:
    [| ?\<pi> : ?P <\<^sub>C\<^sub>F\<^sub>.\<^sub>\<Prod> ?A :
       ?I \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<CC>;
       ?I \<in>\<^sub>\<circ> \<omega> |]
    ==> ?\<pi> :
        ?P <\<^sub>C\<^sub>F\<^sub>.\<^sub>\<Prod>\<^sub>.\<^sub>f\<^sub>i\<^sub>n ?A :
        ?I \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<CC>
theorem
  is_cat_finite_obj_prodD:
    ?\<pi> :
    ?P <\<^sub>C\<^sub>F\<^sub>.\<^sub>\<Prod>\<^sub>.\<^sub>f\<^sub>i\<^sub>n ?A :
    ?I \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<CC> ==>
    ?\<pi> : ?P <\<^sub>C\<^sub>F\<^sub>.\<^sub>\<Prod> ?A :
    ?I \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<CC>
    ?\<pi> :
    ?P <\<^sub>C\<^sub>F\<^sub>.\<^sub>\<Prod>\<^sub>.\<^sub>f\<^sub>i\<^sub>n ?A :
    ?I \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<CC> ==>
    ?I \<in>\<^sub>\<circ> \<omega>
theorem
  is_cat_finite_obj_prodE:
    [| ?\<pi> :
       ?P <\<^sub>C\<^sub>F\<^sub>.\<^sub>\<Prod>\<^sub>.\<^sub>f\<^sub>i\<^sub>n ?A :
       ?I \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<CC>;
       [| ?\<pi> : ?P <\<^sub>C\<^sub>F\<^sub>.\<^sub>\<Prod> ?A :
          ?I \<mapsto>\<mapsto>\<^sub>C\<^bsub>?\<alpha>\<^esub> ?\<CC>;
          ?I \<in>\<^sub>\<circ> \<omega> |]
       ==> ?W |]
